<script type="c2a90bcfe990f1dba4e5d4c5-text/javascript">
    function setCookie(name, value) {
        document.cookie = name + "=" + value;
    }
    function getCookie(name) {
        var r = document.cookie.match("(^|;) ?" + name + "=([^;]*)(;|$)");
        if (r) return r[2];
        else return "";
    }
    function deleteCookie(name) {
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() - 1);
        document.cookie = name += "=; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
    }
    ////
    function getParameterByName() {
        var vars = [], hash;
        var hashes = window.location.href.slice(window.location.href.indexOf('?') + 1).split('&');
        for(var i = 0; i < hashes.length; i++)
        {
            hash = hashes[i].split('=');
            vars.push(hash[0]);
            vars[hash[0]] = hash[1];
        }
        return vars;
    }
                    var source = getCookie('utm_source');
    var medium = getCookie('utm_medium');
    var campaign = getCookie('utm_campaign');
    var keyword = getCookie('utm_keyword');


    // Set the cookies
    if(getCookie('utm_source') == null || getCookie('utm_source') == "" || getCookie('utm_source') == "undefined") {
        setCookie('utm_source', source);
    }
    if(getCookie('utm_medium') == null || getCookie('utm_medium') == "" || getCookie('utm_medium') == "undefined") {
        setCookie('utm_medium', medium);
    }
    if(getCookie('utm_campaign') == null || getCookie('utm_campaign') == "" || getCookie('utm_campaign') == "undefined") {
        setCookie('utm_campaign', campaign);
    }
    if(getCookie('utm_keyword') == null || getCookie('utm_keyword') == "" || getCookie('utm_keyword') == "undefined") {
        setCookie('utm_keyword', keyword);
    }

<script data-cfasync="false">
    (function(){
        var isRoistatReady = false;
        var isChatraReady = false;
        var isDataSet = false;
        var setIntegrationData = function(){
            if (isDataSet || !isRoistatReady || !isChatraReady) {
                return;
                //console.log('data is set');
            }
            Chatra("setIntegrationData", {roistat_visit: window.roistat.visit});
            isDataSet = true;
            console.log('data is true');
        };
        window.onRoistatModuleLoaded = function(){
            window.roistat.registerOnVisitProcessedCallback(function(){
                isRoistatReady = true;
                setIntegrationData();
            });
        };
        window.ChatraSetup = {
            onAnalyticEvent: function(eventName) {
                isChatraReady = true;
                setIntegrationData();
                console.log('chatr ready');
            }
        };
    })();

<script type="c2a90bcfe990f1dba4e5d4c5-text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function($) {
            var DoingTime = 0;
            // cosul pentru animatie a butonului de call  darwin
            bounce_button();
            function aut_of_block(){
                var period = 0;
                period++;
                if (period <=2) {
                    //show tooltip here
                    $('.tooltip_cont').css({'display': 'block'});
                    $('.tooltip_cont').animate({'opacity': 1}, 600);
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        $('.tooltip_cont').animate({
                            'opacity': 0},
                            500, function() {
                            $('.tooltip_cont').css({'display': 'none'});
                        });
                        bounce_button();
                    }, 5000);
                    DoingTime++;
                } else {
                    bounce_button();
                }
            }
            function bounce_button(){
                if (DoingTime < 2) {
                    var Execution = 0;
                    var DoAnim = setInterval(function(){
                            Execution++;
                        if (Execution <= 2) {
                            $('.apel').removeClass('active_roll_call');
                            $('.apel').addClass('bounce_button_active');
                            setTimeout(function(){
                                $('.apel').removeClass('bounce_button_active');
                                $('.apel').addClass('active_roll_call');
                            }, 600);
                        } else{
                            aut_of_block();
                            clearInterval(DoAnim);
                        }
                    }, 2000);
                } else {
                    var DoAnim = setInterval(function(){
                            $('.apel').removeClass('active_roll_call');
                            $('.apel').addClass('bounce_button_active');
                            setTimeout(function(){
                                $('.apel').removeClass('bounce_button_active');
                                $('.apel').addClass('active_roll_call');
                            }, 1200);
                    }, 4000);
                }
            }
        });
    </script>

<script type="c2a90bcfe990f1dba4e5d4c5-text/javascript">
	$(document).on('click','#nl-terms', function (e) {
        if ($(this).find('input:checkbox:checked').length == 1){
            $('.subscribe_newsletter').removeAttr('disabled');
            $('.subscribe_newsletter').css('opacity','1');
        } else {
            $('.subscribe_newsletter').attr("disabled", "disabled");
            $('.subscribe_newsletter').css('opacity','0.5');
        }
    });
    $(document).on("click", ".subscribe_newsletter", function (element) {
        element.preventDefault();
        var form = $(element.target).closest('form');

        var validate = validateErrors(form);

        if(! validate) {
            return false;
        }

        $(element.target).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
        $.ajax({
            url: '/' + lang + '/newsletter/send',
            type: 'POST',
            data: form.serialize(),
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function (data) {
                thanks(data.message , 2);
                form.trigger("reset").find('input').css("border", "");
                $(element.target).attr('disabled', false);
            },
            error: function (resp) {
                $(element.target).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                if (resp.success == false) {
                    validateJson(form, resp.responseJSON.data);
                }
            }
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="c2a90bcfe990f1dba4e5d4c5-text/javascript">
    $(document).on("click", ".get_preorder", function (e) {

        var my_form = $('#preorder-form-modal');

        var name = my_form.find('.d_name').val();
        var phone = my_form.find('.d_phone').val();
        var product_name = $('.title h1').text();
        var product_id = $('.p_id').text();
        var price = $('.buy h2').text();

        if (name && phone) {
            $('button.get_preorder').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            $.ajax({
                url: '/' + lang + '/getDetailsA',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    name: name.trim(),
                    phone: phone.trim(),
                    product_name: product_name.trim(),
                    product_id: product_id.trim(),
                    price: price.trim(),
                    canal: 'preorder'
                },
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function (data) {
                    if (data.success == 'ok') {
                        thanks(data.message, 1);
                        $('button.get_preorder').text(data.message);

                        $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
                    } else {
                        thanks(data.message , 2);
                    }
                },
                error: function (resp) {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                    if (resp.status == 406) {
                        var data = resp.responseJSON.data;
                        $('button.get_preorder').attr('disabled', false);
                        for (var item in data){
                            $(my_form).find("input.d_"+item).css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                            thanks(data[item], 2);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        } else {
            if (name == "" || name == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            if (phone == "" || phone == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
        }
        return true;
    });

        var my_form = $('#tab-credit');

    $(document).on("click", ".get_details", function (e) {

        var my_form = $('#more-info-form-modal');
        var valName = my_form.find('.d_name').val();
        var name = 'Mai multe detalii: ' + my_form.find('.d_name').val();
        var phone = my_form.find('.d_phone').val();
        var product_name = $('.title h1').text();
        var product_id = $('.p_id').text();
        var price = $('.buy h2').text();

        if (valName && phone) {
            $("button.get_details").attr("disabled", true);
            $.ajax({
                url: '/' + lang + '/getDetailsA',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    name: name.trim(),
                    phone: phone.trim(),
                    product_name: product_name.trim(),
                    product_id: product_id.trim(),
                    price: price,
                    canal: 'info'
                },
                dataType: 'json',
                success: function (data) {
                    if (data.success == 'ok') {
                        thanks(data.message, 1);
                        my_form.find('.modal-body').empty().html('<h2>' + data.message + '</h2>');
                        $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                        window.location.hash = '#success-more_details';
                    } else {
                        $(my_form).find("input").css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                        thanks(data.message, 2);
                    }
                },
                error: function (resp) {
                    $(my_form).find('input.d_name, input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710");
                    if (resp.status == 406) {
                        $("button.get_details").attr("disabled", false);
                        var data = resp.responseJSON.data;
                        $('.get_reserve').attr("disabled", false);
                        for (var item in data){
                            $(my_form).find("input.d_"+item).css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024");
                            thanks(data[item], 2);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        } else {

            if (valName == "" || valName == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_name').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            if (phone == "" || phone == undefined){
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #ee4024")
            } else {
                $(my_form).find('input.d_phone').css("border", "solid 1px #5fc710")
            }
            thanks(complete_all_input, 2);
        }
        return true;
    });

            mapPickup.scrollWheelZoom.disable();

            L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png').addTo(mapPickup);

            var dico = L.Icon.extend({
                options: {
                    iconUrl: 'https://darwin.md/img/marker.png',
                    iconSize: [41, 58],
                    iconAnchor: [20, 58],
                    popupAnchor: [1, -60]
                }
            });

            var darwinIcon = new dico();
        }

        if ($('#map-trade-in').length){
            mapTradeIn = L.map('map-trade-in', {dragging: d, attributionControl: false}).setView([47.0045067, 28.8413991], 7);
            mapTradeIn.zoomControl.setPosition('bottomright');
            mapTradeIn.scrollWheelZoom.disable();
            L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png').addTo(mapTradeIn);

            var dico = L.Icon.extend({
                options: {
                    iconUrl: 'https://darwin.md/img/marker.png',
                    iconSize: [41, 58],
                    iconAnchor: [20, 58],
                    popupAnchor: [1, -60]
                }
            });

            var darwinIcon = new dico();
        }

        if ($('#map-trade-in').length || $("#pick-up-map").length){
            jQuery.each(shops, function (c, cityShops) {
                jQuery.each(cityShops, function (i, e) {
                    var location = e["location"].split(",");
                    popupContent = '' +
                        '<div style="width:270px">' +
                        '   <img src="https://darwin.md/img/logo_map.png" class="">   ' +
                        '    <p><span style="font-size:16px;">'+e[city]+' '+e[address]+'</span>' +
                        '       <br><span style="font-size:12px;">'+e[grafic]+'</span><br>' +
                        '       <span style="font-size:16px;"><img src="'+e["phone_img"]+'"></img></span>' +
                        '        <span style="text-decoration:underline; color:#06F;"><img src="'+e["email_img"]+'"></img></span>'+
                        '   </p>' +
                        '</div>';
                    if ($('#pick-up-map').length){
	                    shop_marker_pickup = L.marker([location[0], location[1]], {icon: darwinIcon}).addTo(mapPickup);
	                    shop_marker_pickup.bindPopup(popupContent);
                	};
                    if ($('#map-trade-in').length){
                        shop_marker_trade_in = L.marker([location[0], location[1]], {icon: darwinIcon}).addTo(mapTradeIn);
                        shop_marker_trade_in.bindPopup(popupContent);
                    };
                });
            });
        }



        $(document).on("click", '.sort-by-location', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            let that = this;
            if ($(this).hasClass('sort-pickup')) {
                map = mapPickup;
            }
            if ($(this).hasClass('sort-trade-in')) {
                map = mapTradeIn;
            }

                map.locate();
                map.on('locationfound', function (data) {
                    L.marker([data.latitude, data.longitude]).addTo(map);
                    L.circle([data.latitude, data.longitude], data.accuracy, {
                        weight: 1,
                        color: '#267fca',
                        fillColor: '#267fca',
                        fillOpacity: 0.1
                    }).addTo(map);
                    orderStores(data.latlng , that);
                    user_located = true;
                });
        });

        function orderStores(user_location, that) {
            var $stores;
            var wrapperClass;
            if ($(that).hasClass('sort-pickup')) {
                wrapperClass = ".pick-up-form-wrap";
                var $stores = $('.pick-up-form-wrap .cities .htag');
            }
            if ($(that).hasClass('sort-trade-in')) {
                var $stores = $('.trade-in-wrapper .cities .htag');
                wrapperClass = ".trade-in-wrapper";
            }

            var $locations = $stores.children('a:not(.capital-show-locations, .city-zone, .capital-north-show-locations)');

            $locations.sort(function (a, b) {
                var a_location = {lat: $(a).data('lat'), lng: $(a).data('lng')};
                var b_location = {lat: $(b).data('lat'), lng: $(b).data('lng')};
                var a_distance = haversineDistance(user_location, a_location);
                var b_distance = haversineDistance(user_location, b_location);


                if (a_distance > b_distance) {
                    return 1;
                }
                if (a_distance < b_distance) {
                    return -1;
                }
                return 0;
            });

            if ($($locations[0]).data('category') == "capital"){
                $(wrapperClass + " .capital-show-locations").trigger('click');
                $(wrapperClass + ' a.city-zone[data-zone="'+$($locations[0]).data('zone')+'"]').trigger('click');
            }
            if ($($locations[0]).data('category') == "north-capital"){
                $(wrapperClass + " .capital-north-show-locations").trigger('click');
            }

            $locations.detach().appendTo($stores);
            map.setView([$($locations[0]).data('lat'), $($locations[0]).data('lng')], 13);

            $($locations[0]).trigger('click');
        }

        function haversineDistance(c1 = {}, c2 = {}) {
            var p = 0.017453292519943295;
            var c = Math.cos;
            var a = 0.5 - c((c2.lat - c1.lat) * p) / 2 + c(c1.lat * p) * c(c2.lat * p) * (1 - c((c2.lng - c1.lng) * p)) / 2;
            return 12742 * Math.asin(Math.sqrt(a));
        }

        /*$('.cities .htag a').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            let lat = $(this).data('lat');
            let lng = $(this).data('lng');

            updateMap(lat, lng, this)
        });*/

    function updateMap(c, key, el) {
        var map;
        var shop_marker;
        if ($(el).closest('.htag').first().hasClass('pickup-htag')) {
            map = mapPickup;
            shop_marker = shop_marker_pickup;
        }
        if ($(el).closest('.htag').first().hasClass('trade-in-htag')) {
            map = mapTradeIn;
            shop_marker = shop_marker_trade_in;
        }
        // Add active class to li element
        $(el).parents('.cities').find('a:not(".capital-show-locations")').removeClass('active');
        $(el).addClass('active');
        // Get store by index position
        var store = shops[c][key];
        var location = store["location"].split(",");
        popupContent = '' +
            '<div style="width:230px">' +
            '   <img class="img-fluid" src="https://darwin.md/photos/shares/photo/setting/logo-darwin-black.png " class="">   ' +
            '    <p><span style="font-size:16px;">'+store[city]+' '+store[address]+'</span>' +
            '       <br><span style="font-size:12px;">'+store[grafic]+'</span><br>' +
            '       <span style="font-size:16px;"><img src="'+store.phone_img+'"></img></span>' +
            '        <span style="text-decoration:underline; color:#06F;"><img src="'+store.email_img+'"></img></span>'+
            '   </p>' +
            '</div>';
        // Update map
        shop_marker.setLatLng([location[0], location[1]]).update();
        shop_marker.bindPopup(popupContent).openPopup();
        map.setView([location[0], location[1]], 14);
        map.flyTo([location[0], location[1]]);
    }
</script>

    function addCityStores(city) {
        $(".street select").html("");
        jQuery.each(shops[city], function (i, e) {
            $("<option data-li='" + city + "' data-si='" + i + "' >" + e[address] + "</option>").appendTo(".street select");
        });
    }

    addCityStores("Chi»ôinƒÉu");
    $(".city select").change(function (e) {
        let city = $(this).find("option:selected").data("li");
        addCityStores(city);
    });

<script type="c2a90bcfe990f1dba4e5d4c5-text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
            var timer;
            $('.categories > li').hover(function () {
                let that = this;
                timer = setTimeout(function () {
                    $(".subcategories div.flex-container").addClass("d-none");
                    $(".recommended-side").addClass('d-none');
                    let currentId = $(that).data("id");
                    $(".subcategories div#" + currentId).removeClass('d-none');
                    $(".recommended-side#" + currentId).removeClass('d-none');
                    $('.categories > li').removeClass('showed');
                    $(that).addClass('showed');
                }, 250)
            }, function () {
                clearTimeout(timer);
            });
        });
    </script>
<script type="c2a90bcfe990f1dba4e5d4c5-text/javascript">
        function adaptMenu() {
            /* 	toggle menu on resize */
            $('.rmm').each(function () {
                // initialize vars
                var maxWidth = 0;
                var width = 0;

                // width of menu list (non-toggled)
                $('.rmm-menu').children("li").each(function () {
                    if ($(this).parent().hasClass('rmm-menu')) {
                        width = $(this).outerWidth();//outerWidth();
                        if (width > 0) {
                            maxWidth += width;
                        }
                    }
                });

                // compare width
                var width = $('.rmm').css('max-width');
                width = width.replace('px', '');

                if ($(this).parent().width() > width) {
                    $('.rmm-menu').removeClass("rmm-mobile");

                    //remove all classes from mobile verion
                    $(".rmm-menu ul").removeClass("rmm-subview");
                    $(".rmm-menu li").removeClass("rmm-subover-hidden");
                    $(".rmm-menu li").removeClass("rmm-subover-visible");
                    $(".rmm-menu a").removeClass("rmm-subover-header");

                    $(".rmm-toggled").removeClass("rmm-closed");
                    $('.rmm-toggled').hide();

                    //$('.rmm-toggled').removeClass("rmm-view");
                    //$('.rmm-toggled').addClass("rmm-closed");
                } else {
                    $('.rmm-menu').addClass("rmm-mobile");

                    //$('.rmm-toggled').removeClass("rmm-closed");
                }
            });
        }

        // jQuery(window).load(function () {
        //     responsiveMultiMenu();
        //     adaptMenu();
        // });


        $(window).resize(function () {
            adaptMenu();
        });

    </script>
<script type="c2a90bcfe990f1dba4e5d4c5-text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {

            var lastCategory;
            $(".expandMenu").click(function () {
                $(".expandedMobileMenu").toggleClass("opened");
                $(".menu-first-level").toggleClass("d-none");
                $("body").addClass('fixed-body');
            });
            $(".expandedMobileMenu .closeCat").click(function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass('closeCat')) {
                    $(".expandedMobileMenu").toggleClass("opened");
                    $(".menu-first-level").toggleClass("d-none");
                    $('body').removeClass('fixed-body');
                }
            });
            $(".expandedMobileMenu .eye-item, .expandedMobileMenu .scale-item, .expandedMobileMenu .cart-item").click(function () {
                $("#eye-block, #scale-block, #cart-block").addClass("d-none");
                $(".expandedMobileMenu #" + $(this).data('block')).toggleClass("d-none");
                //$(".closeCat").toggleClass("close-block").toggleClass('closeCat');
                $(".close-container").removeClass("d-none");
                $('.user-item').addClass('d-none');
                $(".currentCategory").text($(this).find('a').attr("title")).removeClass("d-none");
            });
            $(document).on('click', ".close-block", function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass('close-block')) {
                    $("#eye-block, #scale-block, #cart-block").addClass("d-none");
                    $(this).addClass("closeCat").removeClass("close-block");
                }
            });
            $("#openLoginForm").click(function () {
                $('.top-user-login').find('.sign-up-container').toggleClass("d-none");
                //$(".closeCat").toggleClass("close-login").toggleClass('closeCat');
                $('.close-container').removeClass('d-none');
            });
            $(".close-container").click(function () {
                $(".sign-up-container, .products-container").addClass("d-none");
                $(this).addClass('d-none');
                $('.user-item').removeClass('d-none');
                $('.currentCategory').addClass('d-none');
            });
            $(document).on("click", ".close-login", function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass('close-login')) {
                    $(this).addClass("closeCat").removeClass("close-login");
                    $(".top-user-login .sign-up-container").addClass("d-none");
                }
            });

            $(".all-categories-show").click(function () {
                $(".util-links").toggleClass('d-none');
                $(".all-categories").toggleClass("d-none");
                $(".currentCategory").removeClass("d-none").text("Toate categoriile");
                $(".back-to-utils").toggleClass("d-none");
                $(".user-item").addClass('d-none');
                $(".contact-info").addClass('d-none');
                //$(".back-category").toggleClass('d-none')
            });
            $(".back-to-utils").click(function () {
                $(".util-links").removeClass('d-none');
                $(".all-categories").addClass("d-none");
                if ($(".expandedMobileMenu .bubbles").hasClass("d-none")) {
                    $(".top-user-login .sign-up-container").removeClass("d-none");
                    $(".expandedMobileMenu .bubbles").removeClass("d-none").addClass("d-flex");
                    $(".expandedMobileMenu .menu-icon ").addClass("d-flex").removeClass("d-none");
                    //$(".expandedMobileMenu .top").removeClass("justify-content-end");
                }
                if ($(".all-categories").hasClass("d-none")) {
                    $(".rmm-subover-visible").last().find('a').removeClass("rmm-subover-header");
                    $(".rmm-subover-visible").last().find('ul').removeClass("rmm-subview");
                    $(".rmm-subover-visible").last().parent().find("li").removeClass("rmm-subover-hidden");
                    $(".rmm-subover-visible").last().removeClass('rmm-subover-visible');
                }
                $(".contact-info").removeClass('d-none');
                $('.user-item').removeClass('d-none');
                $(".currentCategory").addClass("d-none");
                $(this).toggleClass('d-none');

            });
            $(".all-categories-show").click(function () {
                $(".top-user-login .sign-up-container").addClass("d-none");
                $(".expandedMobileMenu .bubbles").removeClass("d-flex").addClass("d-none");
                $(".expandedMobileMenu .menu-icon ").removeClass("d-flex").addClass("d-none");
                //$(".expandedMobileMenu .top").addClass("justify-content-end");
            });
            $(".rmm-dropdown:not(.from-main)").click(function () {
                lastCategory = $(".currentCategory").text();
                $(".currentCategory").text($(this).text());
                $('.back-to-utils').addClass('d-none');
                $('.back-category').removeClass('d-none');
            });
            $(".rmm-dropdown.from-main").click(function () {
                $(".back-to-utils").toggleClass("d-none");
                $(".user-item").addClass('d-none');
                $(".currentCategory").text($(this).text()).removeClass("d-none");
                $(".contact-info").addClass('d-none');
            });
            $(".back-category").click(function () {
                if ($(".currentCategory").text() == lastCategory) {
                    $(".currentCategory").text("Toate categoriile");
                    $('.back-to-utils').removeClass('d-none');
                    $('.back-category').addClass('d-none');
                } else {
                    $(".currentCategory").text(lastCategory);
                }
                $(".rmm-subover-visible").last().find('a').removeClass("rmm-subover-header");
                $(".rmm-subover-visible").last().find('ul').removeClass("rmm-subview");
                $(".rmm-subover-visible").last().parent().find("li").removeClass("rmm-subover-hidden");
                $(".rmm-subover-visible").last().removeClass('rmm-subover-visible');
            });
        })
        $("#expandMenu").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
        });
    </script>
